<script type="text/javascript">
    require(['viewmodels/journeyCheckFormUi'], function(viewmodel) {
        viewmodel.init({"departureStation":null,"arrivalStation":null,"departureDate":"0001-01-01T00:00:00","isDefined":false});
    });

<script>
    var isMobile = {
        Android: function () { return navigator.userAgent.match(/Android/i); },
        BlackBerry: function () { return navigator.userAgent.match(/BlackBerry/i); },
        iOS: function () { return navigator.userAgent.match(/iPhone|iPad|iPod/i); },
        Opera: function () { return navigator.userAgent.match(/Opera Mini/i); },
        Windows: function () { return navigator.userAgent.match(/IEMobile/i); },
        any: function () { return (isMobile.Android() || isMobile.BlackBerry() || isMobile.iOS() || isMobile.Opera() || isMobile.Windows()); }
    };

    // move jumbo image to parent div
    var bg = null, url = null;
    if (isMobile.any()) {
        bg = document.getElementById("qtt-mobile-image").style.backgroundImage;
    }
    else {
        bg = document.getElementById("qtt__search").style.backgroundImage;
    }

    if (bg) {
        url = bg.substring(4, bg.length - 1);
    }

    if (url) {

        document.getElementById("qtt__search").style.backgroundImage = "";
        document.getElementById("qtt-mobile-image").style.backgroundImage = "";
        document.querySelectorAll('[role="main"]')[0].style.backgroundImage = 'url(' + url + ')';       
    }

    // detect breadcrumb
    var hasBreadcrumb = document.getElementsByClassName('component-breadcrumbs');
    if (hasBreadcrumb.length > 0) {
        document.body.className += " hasBreadcrumb";
    }
    // add QTT class
    var hasQTTwithImage = document.getElementsByClassName('qtt-tabbed--without-image');
    if (hasQTTwithImage.length <= 0) {
        document.body.className += " hasQTTwithImage";
    }
    
</script>
